# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)


Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis of the Grafana three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) implementation. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

### **1. Core Role Definitions**
- `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` - Defines RoleViewer, RoleEditor, RoleAdmin types
- `pkg/services/org/model.go` - Organization-level role definitions

### **2. Role-to-Permission Mapping**
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go` - Contains `DeclareFixedRoles()` that registers the three basic role tiers with their permissions
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go` - Defines Permission model and utilities like `PermissionsForActions()` and `ConcatPermissions()`

### **3. Permission Guard Middleware**
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go` - HTTP middleware that guards endpoints with permission checks
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go` - Implements the Evaluator interface with `EvalPermission()`, `EvalAll()`, and `EvalAny()` functions
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go` - Core AccessControl service with permission evaluation logic

### **4. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance**
- `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go` - Implements `GetInheritedScopes()` for permission inheritance through folder hierarchy
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go` - Folder-specific permission service
- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go` - Dashboard-specific permission service
- `pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go` - Legacy permission types (VIEW, EDIT, ADMIN)

### **5. Authorization Enforcement**
- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go` - RBAC service with `checkPermission()` and `checkInheritedPermissions()` methods
- `pkg/api/folder.go`, `pkg/api/dashboard.go` - API route

1. Role Type Definition (Identity Layer)\\n\\nThe fundamental role types are defined in `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go` with constants RoleViewer, RoleEditor, and RoleAdmin. These are re-exported in `pkg/services/org/model.go` for organization-level management.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\n**Core Definitions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`: Contains `DeclareFixedRoles()` function that registers fixed role definitions and `BasicRolePrefix` constant ('basic:') for role naming\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go`: Defines the `Permission` struct and provides `PermissionsForActions()` and `ConcatPermissions()` utility functions for creating permission sets\\n\\n**Role Registration:**\\nThe `DeclareFixedRoles()` function in roles.go registers three basic roles:\\n- `basic_viewer`: View-only permissions (folders:read, dashboards:read, etc.)\\n- `basic_editor`: Edit permissions (folders:write, dashboards:write, etc.)\\n- `basic_admin`: Admin permissions (folders.permissions:write, dashboards.permissions:write, etc.)\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\n**Middleware Stack:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go`: Implements the `Middleware()` function that wraps HTTP handlers with permission checking. It evaluates permissions using the AccessControl interface.\\n- `pkg/middleware/auth.go`: Contains higher-level authentication and authorization middleware including role-based protection\\n\\n**Permission Evaluation:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go`: Defines the `Evaluator` interface and implements permission checking logic:\\n  - `EvalPermission()`: Creates an evaluator for a specific action and scope\\n  - `EvalAll()`: Requires all conditions to pass (AND logic)\\n  - `EvalAny()`: Requires at least one condition to pass (OR logic)\\n  - `Evaluate()`: Method that checks if a user's permissions satisfy the evaluator\\n\\n**Core Authorization:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/accesscontrol.go`: Implements the `AccessControl` interface with `Evaluate()` and `HasAccess()` functions that orchestrate permission checking\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go`: Implements RBAC authorization with `checkPermission()` and `checkInheritedPermissions()` methods for detailed permission evaluation\\n\\n## 4. Folder and Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\n**Folder Permissions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go`: Implements `FolderPermissionsService` via `ProvideFolderPermissions()`, defines folder-specific actions (ActionFoldersRead, ActionFoldersWrite, ActionFoldersPermissionsWrite)\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go`: Folder service implementation with permission enforcement on create/read/update/delete operations\\n- `pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder_unifiedstorage.go`: Unified storage implementation handling folder permissions\\n\\n**Dashboard Permissions:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go`: Implements `DashboardPermissionsService` via `ProvideDashboardPermissions()`, defines dashboard-specific actions\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/models.go`: Dashboard and folder model definitions\\n\\n**Inherited Scopes (Permission Inheritance):**\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go`: Implements `GetInheritedScopes()` function that traverses the folder hierarchy and returns all parent folder scopes for a dashboard, enabling permission inheritance from folders to dashboards\\n- `pkg/services/searchV2/auth.go`: Uses inherited scopes to filter search results based on hierarchical permissions\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/permissions/dashboard.go`: Database layer that implements permission filtering for dashboards considering folder inheritance\\n\\n**Permission Types:**\\n- `pkg/services/dashboards/dashboardaccess/dashboard_access.go`: Defines legacy permission types:\\n  - `PERMISSION_VIEW` (1)\\n  - `PERMISSION_EDIT` (2)\\n  - `PERMISSION_ADMIN` (4)\\n\\n## 5. Resource-Specific Permission Management\\n\\n**Resource Permission Service:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/service.go`: Implements generic resource permission management with `SetUserPermission()`, `SetTeamPermission()`, `SetBuiltInRolePermission()` methods\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/api.go`: REST API endpoints for managing resource permissions\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/models.go`: Data models for resource permission operations\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/options.go`: Configuration options for resource permission services\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resourcepermissions/store.go`: In-memory and database storage for action sets and permissions\\n\\n**Scope Resolution:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/resolvers.go`: Implements `ScopeAttributeResolver` interface for resolving scope references (e.g., 'folders:uid:xxx' to actual folder scopes)\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/database/database.go`: Database queries for retrieving user/team/role permissions\\n\\n## 6. API Route Protection\\n\\n**Folder API:**\\n- `pkg/api/folder.go`: Registers folder API routes with permission guards using `EvalPermission(dashboards.ActionFoldersRead, uidScope)` and similar evaluators\\n\\n**Dashboard API:**\\n- `pkg/api/dashboard.go`: Registers dashboard API routes with permission guards checking read/write/delete/admin permissions\\n- `pkg/api/dashboard_permission.go`: Dashboard permission management endpoints\\n\\n**Folder Permission API:**\\n- `pkg/api/folder_permission.go`: Folder-specific permission management endpoints\\n\\n**Core Access Control Configuration:**\\n- `pkg/api/accesscontrol.go`: Declares global access control roles and permissions\\n\\n## 7. Supporting Authorization Systems\\n\\n**Library Elements Guard:**\\n- `pkg/services/libraryelements/guard.go`: Permission guards for library elements using `EvalPermission()` with folder access checks\\n\\n**Dashboard Authorization:**\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/authorizer.go`: API server authorizer for dashboards\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/dashboard/sub_dto.go`: Dashboard access information provider\\n\\n**Alert Rules Access Control:**\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/accesscontrol/rules.go`: Alert rules permission enforcement using folder-based scopes\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/accesscontrol/silences.go`: Silence management with folder-scoped permissions\\n\\n**Service Implementation:**\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/service.go`: Core access control service implementation\\n- `pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/receivers.go`: Permission management for alert notification receivers\\n\\nThe architecture implements a hierarchical permission model where folder permissions are inherited by contained dashboards, and all permission decisions flow through a central evaluation engine that checks user permissions against required actions and scopes.\"\n}\n",
